--=-GX36tkxUP6r0NpkDd37h
Content-Type: text/plain
Content-Transfer-Encoding: 7bit

Hello, I've just put together a package (attached) for integrating
System.Drawing with Gtk#. It installs both the C-addon for libdgiplus
and gtk-drawing.dll. README follows:

This packages provides basic System.Drawing integration with GTK#.
Use like this (add -r gtk-drawing to mcs):
Graphics g = GtkDrawing.GtkDrawing.GraphicsFromDrawable
(mywidget.GdkWindow);

If you make a custom widget (like a subclass of DrawingArea), remember
to add:
widget.DoubleBuffered = false;

(This is for the expose event to work properly).

I think it's also necessary to reinitialize the graphics each time the
widget
is configured.
--Artem
